Actor BFG10KGeneralWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
	Ready:
		BG2G AAA 1 A_WeaponReady
		BG2G BBB 1 A_WeaponReady
		BG2G CCC 1 A_WeaponReady
		BG2G DDD 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		BG2G E 13 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/charge15k")

		BG2G GHIJ 1

		BG2G K 1 Bright

Actor DTDevastatorZombieWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
	Ready:
		DEVG A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		DEVG B 10 A_PlaySound("devastator/charge")
		DEVG CDEF 10 Bright
		DEVG G 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG H 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG I 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG G 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG H 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG I 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG G 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG H 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG I 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG G 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG H 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG I 4 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG G 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG H 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG I 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG G 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG H 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG I 3 Bright //A_FireBullets(4,4,2,6,"DevPuff",0,64)
		DEVG A 0 //A_Refire
		DEVG J 3 Bright A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 //A_Recoil(20)
		DEVG J 1 Bright A_Playsound("devastator/fire")
		DEVG K 10 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("ZombieDevastatorBall")
		DEVG L 7 Bright
		DEVG A 50
		Goto Ready
	Flash:
		NULL A 5 A_Light1
		NULL A 10 A_Light2
		NULL A 7 A_Light1
		NULL A 5 A_Light0
		Stop
	}

Actor EraserZombieWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
	Ready:
		RDTI AAAABBBBCCCCBBBB 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlayWeaponSound("Cardinal/9k")
		RDTF C 2 Bright Radius_Quake(1,2,0,1,0)
		RDTF DE 2 Bright Radius_Quake(2,2,0,1,0)
		RDTF FGH 2 Bright Radius_Quake(4,2,0,1,0)
		RDTF IJK 2 Bright Radius_Quake(6,3,0,1,0)
		RDTF L 18 Bright Radius_Quake(8,3,0,1,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash	
		RDTF M 2 Bright Radius_Quake(10,4,0,1,0)
		TNT1 A 0 //A_Recoil(10)	
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(12,6,0,1,0)
		RDTF N 2 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("ZombieDTBFG10KBall",0,1,0,0)	
		RDTF OP 1 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		RDTF QRST 2 //Bright
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(3,10,0,1,0)
		RDTE A 58
		Goto Ready
	}
}

Actor Hexa-ShotgunZombieWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
  States
  {
  Ready:
    HSGN A 1 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Fire:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1,"Reload")
  HexaFire:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/hsgfire")
	TNT1 A 0 A_AlertMonsters
	TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(2)
    TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
    TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(10,5,0,1,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken", 3)
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAA 0 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,0)
    HS4F A 1 Bright A_FireBullets(15.4,10.6,78,Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
    HS4F A 1 Bright 
    HS4F B 2 Bright A_Light2
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
	HSGN CFG 1
	HSGN H 2
	HSER A 3
	HSER B 6
	HSGN GFEDC 2
	Goto ReloadSixShells+3
  AltFire:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",3,"Reload")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",2,"FireLower")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1,"FireMiddle")
	Goto FireUpper
  FireLower:
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgdoublefire")	
    TNT1 A 0 A_AlertMonsters
    TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
    TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(3,3,0,1,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	TNT1 AAAAAA 0 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,0)
    HSGF E 2 Bright A_FireBullets(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff") 
	HSGF F 2 Bright A_Light2
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
	HSRC ABCDE 1
	HSGN A 1
    Goto Ready
  FireUpper:
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgdoublefire")	
    TNT1 A 0 A_AlertMonsters
    TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
    TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(3,3,0,1,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	TNT1 AAAAAA 0 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,0)
    HSGF A 2 Bright A_FireBullets(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
	HSGF B 2 Bright A_Light2
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
	HSRC ABCDE 1
	HSGN A 1
    Goto Ready
  FireMiddle:
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgdoublefire")	
    TNT1 A 0 A_AlertMonsters
    TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
    TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(3,3,0,1,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	TNT1 AAAAAA 0 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,0)
    HSGF C 2 Bright A_FireBullets(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
	HSGF D 2 Bright A_Light2
	TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
	HSRC ABCDE 1
	HSGN A 1
    Goto Ready
  Reload:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",3,"ReloadSixShells")
  	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",2,"ReloadFourShells")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1,"ReloadTwoShells")
	Goto Ready
  ReloadSixShells:
	HSGN SRQ 2
	HSGN PJ 1
	HSGN K 1
	TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SSGShellCasing",25,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(-3,-6),Random(3,6),0)
	HSGN L 1
	HSGR A 12 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgopen")
	HSGR B 1
	HSGR CD 2
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	HSGR E 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")
	HSGR F 3
	HSGR G 2
	HSGR H 1
	HSGR I 8
	HSGR JK 1
	HSGR LM 2
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	HSGR N 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")
	HSGR O 3
	HSGR P 2
	HSGR Q 1
	HSGR R 8
	HSGR ST 1
	HSGR U 2
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	HSGR V 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")	
	HSGR W 3
	HSGR X 2
	HSGR Y 1
	HSGN MNO 1
	HSGN P 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgclose")
	HSGN QRS 2
	HSGN A 2
    Goto Ready
  ReloadFourShells:
	HSGN SRQ 2
	HSGN P 1
	HSEX A 1
	HSEX B 1
	TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SSGShellCasing",25,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(-3,-6),Random(3,6),0)

	HSGR LM 2
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	HSGR N 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")

	HSGR P 2
	HSGR Q 1
	HSGR RS 1
	HSGR TU 2
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("Hexa-ZombieToken",1)
	HSGR V 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")	
	HSGR W 3
	HSGR X 2
	HSGR Y 1
	HSGN MNO 1
	HSGN P 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgclose")
	HSGN QRS 2
	HSGN A 2
	Goto Ready
  ReloadTwoShells:
	HSGN SRQ 2
	HSGN P 1
	HSEX A 1
	HSEX B 1
	TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SSGShellCasing",25,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(-3,-6),Random(3,6),0)
	HSEX C 1
	HSGR Q 12 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgopen")

	HSGR Y 1
	HSGN MNO 1
	HSGN P 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgclose")
	HSGN QRS 2
	HSGN A 2
	Goto Ready
    }

		BTEK AAA 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK AAA 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK AAA 1 Bright A_WeaponReady

		BTEK BB 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK BB 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK CC 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK CC 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK DD 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK DD 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK EE 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		BTEK EE 1 Bright A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 Bright Radius_Quake(4,2,0,1,0)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_Light1
		BTKF A 2 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("LegendaryProjectile",Random(100,-100)/100.00)
		BTKF B 1 Bright A_Light2
		BTKF B 1 Bright A_PlayWeaponSound("BlueDTRFire")
		BTKF C 2 Bright A_Light0
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("LDemonMagazine", 2, 1)
		Goto AltFire
		TNT1 A 0 A_Refire
		Goto Ready		
	AltFire:
  	 TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("LDemonMagazine",50,"Ready")
     BTKR AB 2 Bright
	 BTKR C 3 Bright
	 BTKR D 4 Bright A_PlaySound("weapons/demontecheject")
	 TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(2,2,0,1,0)
	 BTKR E 2 Bright A_PlaySound("weapons/demontechsteam")
	 BTKR F 2 Bright Radius_Quake(2,2,0,1,0)
	 BTKR GHI 2 Bright Radius_Quake(2,2,0,1,0)
	 BTKR J 3 Bright //A_FireCustomMissile("LDemonTechEmptyMag", 0, 0, 0, 1)
	 BTKR K 15 Bright
	 BTKR LMN 2	Bright 
     BTKR O 6 Bright A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/demontechload")
     BTKR O 4 Bright A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/demontechclick")
	 TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("LDemonMagazine", 50)
     BTKR CB 3 Bright
	 BTKR A 2 Bright
	Goto Ready
	}
}

		LMAF A 1 Bright A_FireBullets(22.5,18.3,4,Random(5,15)*6,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		LMAF B 1 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		LMAG BCDE 1 Bright
		LMAG FA 2 Bright
		Goto Ready
    AltFire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ASGZAmmo", 1, 1)
		Goto Ready
    	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoPain", 1)		
		LMAR ABCDEF 1 Bright
		LMAR GO 2 Bright
		LMAR N 2 Bright A_PlaySound("lasgguy/asgout")
		LMAR H 3 Bright
		LMAR I 2 Bright
		LMAR JKL 1 Bright
		LMAR M 35 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("LegendaryEmptyDrumSpawner", 0, 0, 10, 1) 
		LMAR LKJ 1 Bright
		LMAR I 2 Bright

		LMAR P 6 Bright A_PlayWeaponSound("lasgguy/asgin")
		LMAR NOG 2 Bright
		LMAR FEDCBA 1 Bright
		LMAG A 3 Bright
		LMAG A 5 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoPain", 0)
		Goto Ready
	}

Actor FreezerZombieWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
  Ready:
    RIPE A 0 A_StopSound(CHAN_WEAPON)
    RIPR ABCD 4 A_WeaponReady
    Loop
  Fire:
    RIPE A 0 A_GunFlash
    TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/iceshot",6,5)
	RIPE A 2 A_FireCustomMissile("NewZombieFreezeBlast", 0,0, 4,0)
    RIPE B 2 
	RIPE C 2 
	TNT1 D 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/chill",5,1.0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Refire
	RIPE EFGHI 6 A_WeaponReady
    Goto Ready
  AltFire:
